{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01KSBRqdymxLFkZxx8tE6vNW","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_016MUtBBVPioN5TuB8PY8F4K","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Envoy External Processing Filter Migration Guide: v1.30 → v1.31\n\n**Version Date**: July 2024\n**API Version**: v3\n**Filter Name**: `envoy.filters.http.ext_proc`\n\n---\n\n## Overview\n\nThe External Processing (ext_proc) HTTP filter in Envoy v1.31 introduces several significant enhancements focused on improving route cache management and observability. This migration guide covers the changes from Envoy v1.30.0 (April 2024) to v1.31.0 (July 2024).\n\n**Key Changes Summary:**\n- New `route_cache_action` field provides flexible route cache management\n- Introduction of `observability_mode` for non-blocking external processor communication\n- Support for `deferred_close_timeout` to manage gRPC stream lifecycle in observability mode\n- Breaking change: `disable_clear_route_cache` is now promoted into a oneof with `route_cache_action`\n- Behavioral change: Timeout errors now return 504 Gateway Timeout instead of 500 Internal Server Error\n\n---\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n### 1. Route Cache Management Field Promotion\n\n**Impact**: Configurations using `disable_clear_route_cache` with non-default values alongside `route_cache_action` will fail validation.\n\n**What Changed:**\n- The `disable_clear_route_cache` (field 11) field is now being promoted into a oneof group called `clear_route_cache_type`\n- A new field `route_cache_action` (field 18) is introduced as the preferred way to manage route cache behavior\n- Only ONE of these fields can be set to a non-default value\n\n**Proto Definition (v1.31):**\n\n```protobuf\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  // NEW: RouteCacheAction enum\n  enum RouteCacheAction {\n    DEFAULT = 0;      // Default behavior - clear cache only when set in response\n    CLEAR = 1;        // Always clear route cache\n    RETAIN = 2;       // Never clear route cache\n  }\n\n  // DEPRECATED (but still functional): Sets route cache action to RETAIN\n  bool disable_clear_route_cache = 11\n      [(udpa.annotations.field_migrate).oneof_promotion = \"clear_route_cache_type\"];\n\n  // NEW: Replaces disable_clear_route_cache functionality\n  RouteCacheAction route_cache_action = 18\n      [(udpa.annotations.field_migrate).oneof_promotion = \"clear_route_cache_type\"];\n}\n```\n\n**Migration Steps:**\n\n1. **Identify Current Configuration**:\n   ```yaml\n   # v1.30 configuration\n   ext_proc:\n     grpc_service:\n       envoy_grpc:\n         cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n     disable_clear_route_cache: true\n   ```\n\n2. **Update to v1.31**:\n   ```yaml\n   # v1.31 configuration - Option A: Use new route_cache_action field\n   ext_proc:\n     grpc_service:\n       envoy_grpc:\n         cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n     route_cache_action: RETAIN  # Replaces disable_clear_route_cache: true\n   ```\n\n3. **Backward Compatibility**:\n   - The old `disable_clear_route_cache: true` setting is automatically converted to `route_cache_action: RETAIN`\n   - The old `disable_clear_route_cache: false` (or omitted) maps to `route_cache_action: DEFAULT`\n\n**Validation Errors:**\n```\nConfiguration Error: \"disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not\nbe set to none-default at the same time.\"\n```\n\nThis error occurs when both are specified with non-default values. **Remove the old field and use the new one instead.**\n\n**Best Practice:**\n- Always use `route_cache_action` in new configurations\n- Only use `disable_clear_route_cache` if you must maintain v1.30 compatibility\n\n---\n\n## Deprecated Features\n\n### 1. `async_mode` Field (Already Unimplemented)\n\n**Status**: Deprecated in favor of `observability_mode`\n\n**Background:**\n- `async_mode` was reserved in v1.30 as `reserved 4; reserved \"async_mode\";`\n- It was never implemented and marked with `[#not-implemented-hide:]`\n\n**What's Changing:**\n- v1.31 introduces `observability_mode` as the official mechanism for non-blocking external processor communication\n- `observability_mode` supersedes the planned (but never implemented) `async_mode`\n\n**Migration Path:**\n- If you have any references to `async_mode`, ignore them or remove them\n- Use `observability_mode` instead for \"send and go\" communication patterns\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### 1. Route Cache Action Enum\n\n**Purpose**: Provides explicit control over when route caches are cleared based on external processor responses.\n\n**Field Details:**\n- Field Number: 18 (in ExternalProcessor message)\n- Type: Enum (ExternalProcessor.RouteCacheAction)\n- Default: DEFAULT\n- Applies to: Request header processing responses\n\n**Enum Values:**\n\n| Value | Behavior | Use Case |\n|-------|----------|----------|\n| **DEFAULT** | Clear route cache only when the external processor explicitly sets `clear_route_cache: true` in the response | Normal operation - processor controls cache invalidation |\n| **CLEAR** | Always clear the route cache regardless of processor response | When header mutations might affect routing decisions; ensures fresh route computation |\n| **RETAIN** | Never clear the route cache regardless of processor response | When processor modifications don't affect routing; improves performance |\n\n**Configuration Example:**\n\n```yaml\n# Force route cache clearing on header mutations\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  route_cache_action: CLEAR\n\n# Or use the legacy form that auto-converts\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  disable_clear_route_cache: true  # Maps to RETAIN\n```\n\n**Behavioral Details:**\n- Route cache action is evaluated after the external processor responds to request headers\n- The action only applies to header processing responses, not body or trailer responses\n- Setting this field overrides any `clear_route_cache` field in the processor response (when not DEFAULT)\n\n**Implementation Location:**\n- Source: `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` (lines 186-187, 213-221)\n- Proto: `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 232-258)\n\n---\n\n### 2. Observability Mode\n\n**Purpose**: Enables \"Send and Go\" mode where the external processor observes traffic without blocking request/response processing.\n\n**Field Details:**\n- Field Number: 17 (in ExternalProcessor message)\n- Type: Boolean\n- Default: false\n- Proto Location: `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 221-243)\n\n**Configuration Example:**\n\n```yaml\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 5000ms  # Optional: defaults to 5 seconds\n```\n\n**Behavior When Enabled:**\n\n1. **Non-Blocking Communication**: Each part of the HTTP request or response specified by `ProcessingMode` is sent to the external processor without pausing filter chain iteration\n2. **No Waiting for Responses**: Envoy doesn't wait for responses from the external processor; any responses received are ignored\n3. **Stream Closure**: The external processor can still close the stream to indicate it needs no more messages\n4. **Limited Body Processing**: Only STREAMED body processing mode is fully supported; other body modes (BUFFERED, BUFFERED_PARTIAL) will be ignored, but NONE mode (skip body) works as expected\n5. **Timeout Management**: The `message_timeout` field doesn't apply in observability mode since responses aren't awaited\n\n**Important Constraints:**\n\n- ✅ Request headers will be sent in observability mode\n- ✅ Response headers will be sent in observability mode\n- ✅ Request/response bodies will be sent in STREAMED mode without waiting\n- ✅ Trailers will be sent if configured\n- ✅ The external processor can close the stream at any time\n- ❌ The external processor must NOT send back responses (they'll be ignored)\n- ❌ Header mutations from processor responses cannot be applied (no responses expected)\n- ❌ Response modifications are not possible (body/header/trailer mutations cannot be applied)\n\n**Use Cases:**\n\n```yaml\n# Observability use case 1: Traffic monitoring\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: monitoring_service\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED\n    response_body_mode: STREAMED\n\n# Observability use case 2: Non-blocking audit logging\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: audit_service\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n```\n\n**Flow Control Warning:**\n\n⚠️ **Important**: Flow control mechanisms to prevent fast senders from overwhelming the slow external processor are still under development (tracked in GitHub issue #33319). Use observability mode with caution in high-throughput environments and consider:\n- Implementing backpressure at the processor\n- Monitoring processor queue depths\n- Using circuit breakers if processor falls behind\n\n**Implementation Location:**\n- Source: `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` (lines 186, 430, 657, 683, 738, 881)\n- Proto: `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 221-243)\n\n---\n\n### 3. Deferred Close Timeout\n\n**Purpose**: Controls how long gRPC streams remain open after the HTTP stream completes in observability mode.\n\n**Field Details:**\n- Field Number: 19 (in ExternalProcessor message)\n- Type: google.protobuf.Duration\n- Default: 5000ms (5 seconds)\n- Valid Range: 0ms to 3600s\n- Proto Location: `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 260-265)\n\n**Configuration Example:**\n\n```yaml\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 3s        # 3 seconds\n  # OR\n  deferred_close_timeout: 10000ms   # 10 seconds\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n1. **When observability mode is enabled**, gRPC streams may remain open longer than the HTTP stream lifetime\n2. **Deferred closure**: When the HTTP request/response completes, Envoy doesn't immediately close the gRPC stream\n3. **Timeout application**: Instead, Envoy sets a timer that will close the stream after `deferred_close_timeout` expires\n4. **Early closure**: The external processor can close the stream earlier by closing its end\n5. **Processing window**: The external processor has `deferred_close_timeout` duration to finish processing any buffered messages\n\n**Use Cases:**\n\n```yaml\n# Short timeout for low-latency services\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 100ms\n\n# Long timeout for batch processors\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 30s\n\n# Match to external processor processing SLA\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 5s\n```\n\n**Implementation Details:**\n- Default constant: `DEFAULT_DEFERRED_CLOSE_TIMEOUT_MS = 5000` (source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h:150)\n- Managed by: `ThreadLocalStreamManager` class for per-stream lifecycle management\n- Triggered in: `DeferredDeletableStream::deferredClose()` method\n\n---\n\n## Configuration Updates\n\n### Complete Configuration Example: v1.30 → v1.31\n\n**v1.30 Configuration:**\n\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n      response_header_mode: SEND\n      request_body_mode: BUFFERED\n    failure_mode_allow: false\n    message_timeout: 200ms\n    disable_clear_route_cache: true\n    stat_prefix: \"my_ext_proc_\"\n```\n\n**v1.31 Configuration (Recommended):**\n\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n      response_header_mode: SEND\n      request_body_mode: BUFFERED\n    failure_mode_allow: false\n    message_timeout: 200ms\n    route_cache_action: RETAIN          # Changed from disable_clear_route_cache\n    stat_prefix: \"my_ext_proc_\"\n    # Optional: new features in v1.31\n    # observability_mode: false         # Defaults to false (blocking mode)\n    # deferred_close_timeout: 5000ms    # Defaults to 5 seconds\n```\n\n**v1.31 Configuration (with Observability Mode):**\n\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n      response_header_mode: SEND\n      request_body_mode: STREAMED       # STREAMED when using observability mode\n    failure_mode_allow: false\n    observability_mode: true             # Enable observability/audit mode\n    deferred_close_timeout: 3s            # Custom timeout\n    stat_prefix: \"audit_proc_\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Behavioral Changes\n\n### 1. Timeout Error Status Code\n\n**Change**: Timeout errors in external processor now return **504 Gateway Timeout** instead of **500 Internal Server Error**.\n\n**Impact**:\n- Clients can distinguish between ext_proc timeouts and other server errors\n- Load balancers can handle 504 differently (retry, failover, etc.)\n- Better observability and error tracking\n\n**Example:**\n\n```\nv1.30 Behavior: ext_proc timeout → 500 Internal Server Error\nv1.31 Behavior: ext_proc timeout → 504 Gateway Timeout\n```\n\n**Affected Scenarios:**\n- Request headers timeout while waiting for processor response\n- Request body timeout\n- Response headers timeout\n- Response body timeout\n\n**Log/Metric Changes:**\n- The metric `ext_proc.message_timeouts` counter remains the same\n- HTTP status code in access logs will change to 504\n\n---\n\n### 2. gRPC Tracing Context Propagation\n\n**Change** (Minor): Tracing context headers are now properly propagated in bidirectional gRPC streams.\n\n**Context**: Both Envoy gRPC and Google C++ gRPC clients now propagate tracing context when calling external services like ext_proc.\n\n**Impact on ext_proc**:\n- Tracing spans from the external processor request can now be correlated with the main request trace\n- Better observability when using distributed tracing\n- External processor traces will show up in trace collection systems\n\n---\n\n## Migration Steps\n\n### Step 1: Review Current Configuration\n\nCheck if your configuration uses `disable_clear_route_cache`:\n\n```bash\n# Search for disable_clear_route_cache in your config\ngrep -r \"disable_clear_route_cache\" /path/to/configs/\n```\n\n### Step 2: Update Route Cache Management\n\n**If using `disable_clear_route_cache: true`:**\n```diff\n- disable_clear_route_cache: true\n+ route_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**If using `disable_clear_route_cache: false` or omitting it:**\n```yaml\n# No change needed, but explicitly setting is clearer:\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT\n```\n\n### Step 3: Plan for New Features\n\nDecide if your use case benefits from the new features:\n\n- **Observability Mode**: Do you have monitoring/audit requirements? Enable with `observability_mode: true`\n- **Timeout Handling**: Are your external processors fast? Consider reducing `deferred_close_timeout`\n- **Explicit Route Cache Control**: Should you use CLEAR instead of relying on processor responses?\n\n### Step 4: Test Migration\n\n```yaml\n# Test configuration with new field\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  route_cache_action: RETAIN     # New field\n  # Keep other settings same\n```\n\n**Validation Checklist:**\n- [ ] Configuration loads without errors\n- [ ] HTTP requests flow through ext_proc normally\n- [ ] Route caching behavior matches expectations\n- [ ] Metrics and logs show expected behavior\n- [ ] Error responses have correct status codes\n\n### Step 5: Deploy to Staging\n\n- Deploy v1.31 to a staging environment\n- Run integration tests\n- Verify with production-like traffic patterns\n- Monitor error rates and latency\n\n### Step 6: Production Rollout\n\n- Roll out gradually using canary deployments\n- Monitor metrics:\n  - `ext_proc.message_timeouts` (should match v1.30)\n  - HTTP 504 responses (previously 500)\n  - Route cache invalidation rate\n- Have rollback plan ready\n\n---\n\n## Testing Recommendations\n\n### 1. Configuration Validation Tests\n\n```yaml\n# Test 1: Verify route_cache_action: CLEAR works\ntest_config:\n  route_cache_action: CLEAR\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\nexpected_behavior: \"Route cache cleared on header mutation\"\n\n# Test 2: Verify route_cache_action: RETAIN works\ntest_config:\n  route_cache_action: RETAIN\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\nexpected_behavior: \"Route cache never cleared\"\n\n# Test 3: Verify error on conflicting config\ntest_config:\n  disable_clear_route_cache: true\n  route_cache_action: CLEAR\nexpected_behavior: \"Configuration error thrown\"\n```\n\n### 2. Observability Mode Tests\n\n```yaml\n# Test 4: Request/response streaming without blocking\ntest_config:\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED\n    response_body_mode: STREAMED\nexpected_behavior: |\n  - Filter doesn't wait for processor responses\n  - Request completes even if processor slow\n  - Processor messages sent asynchronously\n\n# Test 5: Deferred closure timeout\ntest_config:\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 1s\nexpected_behavior: |\n  - Stream closes after 1 second\n  - Processor has 1 second to finish\n  - No messages sent after timeout\n```\n\n### 3. Error Handling Tests\n\n```yaml\n# Test 6: Timeout returns 504\ntest_config:\n  message_timeout: 100ms\n  grpc_service: # Simulated slow service\nexpected_behavior: \"HTTP 504 Gateway Timeout returned\"\n\n# Test 7: Observability mode ignores responses\ntest_config:\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\nexpected_behavior: |\n  - Processor response mutations ignored\n  - Stream continues normally\n  - No header modifications applied\n```\n\n### 4. Integration Test Scenario\n\n```python\n# Pseudo-test code for integration testing\ndef test_ext_proc_v131_migration():\n    # Start v1.31 Envoy with new config\n    envoy = start_envoy(config_v131)\n\n    # Test 1: Normal operation unchanged\n    assert make_request(\"/api\").status == 200\n\n    # Test 2: Route cache action works\n    assert route_cache_cleared() == False  # With RETAIN\n\n    # Test 3: Observability mode non-blocking\n    with slow_processor(delay=5s):\n        start_time = time()\n        response = make_request(\"/api\")\n        elapsed = time() - start_time\n        assert elapsed < 1s  # Didn't wait for processor\n        assert response.status == 200\n\n    # Test 4: Timeout returns 504\n    with failing_processor():\n        response = make_request(\"/api\", timeout=1s)\n        assert response.status == 504\n```\n\n---\n\n## Rollback Guidance\n\n### Rollback to v1.30\n\nIf you encounter issues with v1.31, here's how to safely rollback:\n\n### Step 1: Prepare Fallback Configuration\n\nKeep a v1.30 compatible configuration ready:\n\n```yaml\n# v1.30 compatible configuration\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n  disable_clear_route_cache: true  # Use old field name\n  message_timeout: 200ms\n```\n\n### Step 2: Identify Issues\n\nCheck logs for error patterns:\n\n```bash\n# Configuration validation errors\ngrep \"disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action\" envoy.log\n\n# Timeout errors (now 504 instead of 500)\ngrep \"504 Gateway Timeout\" envoy_access.log\n\n# Observability mode issues (if enabled)\ngrep \"observability_mode\" envoy.log | grep ERROR\n```\n\n### Step 3: Rollback Procedure\n\n1. **Update configuration** to use old `disable_clear_route_cache` field\n2. **Redeploy Envoy v1.30** or pin to v1.31 with backward-compatible config\n3. **Verify traffic** flows normally\n4. **Monitor metrics** to ensure stability\n\n### Step 4: Prevent Recurrence\n\nAfter rollback:\n1. Identify root cause\n2. File issues if bugs found\n3. Plan retry after fixes\n4. Test more thoroughly in staging\n\n### Critical Rollback Indicators\n\n```\nImmediate rollback if:\n- Configuration won't load with \"cannot be set to none-default at the same time\" error\n- 504 responses breaking downstream systems (incompatible with 500)\n- Observability mode preventing normal traffic flow\n- gRPC connection failures to ext_proc\n```\n\n---\n\n## Common Issues and Solutions\n\n### Issue 1: Configuration Validation Error\n\n**Error Message:**\n```\n\"disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set to none-default at the same time.\"\n```\n\n**Cause**: Both fields set with non-default values\n\n**Solution**:\n```yaml\n# Remove the old field\n- disable_clear_route_cache: true\n+ route_cache_action: RETAIN\n\n# Or use only one field\n# Use route_cache_action: DEFAULT  (or omit it)\n# And remove disable_clear_route_cache\n```\n\n### Issue 2: Route Cache Not Clearing When Expected\n\n**Symptom**: Routes aren't being recalculated after header changes\n\n**Diagnosis**:\n```\nCheck setting:\n- route_cache_action: RETAIN → Cache never clears (expected)\n- route_cache_action: DEFAULT → Cache clears only if processor sets clear_route_cache\n- route_cache_action: CLEAR → Cache always clears (ensure this is used)\n```\n\n**Solution**:\n```yaml\n# If header mutations should affect routing\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR\n\n# If you want processor to control cache clearing\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT\n# AND processor must set clear_route_cache: true in response\n```\n\n### Issue 3: Observability Mode Not Sending Messages\n\n**Symptom**: Processor doesn't receive request/response messages\n\n**Diagnosis**:\n```\nCheck:\n1. observability_mode: true is set\n2. processing_mode has appropriate send modes (not all SKIP)\n3. deferred_close_timeout is reasonable\n```\n\n**Solution**:\n```yaml\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND      # Must be SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND     # Must be SEND\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED    # Use STREAMED, not NONE\n    response_body_mode: STREAMED\n```\n\n### Issue 4: Observability Mode Responses Being Ignored\n\n**Symptom**: Processor responses causing mutations but nothing happens\n\n**Expected Behavior**:\n```\nIn observability mode:\n- Processor responses are IGNORED\n- No headers/body/trailer mutations applied\n- No mode_override processed\n- No immediate_response sent\n```\n\n**Solution**:\nUse observability mode ONLY for monitoring/audit. For actual request modification:\n```yaml\n# For modifying requests/responses\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: false        # Use blocking mode\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n  message_timeout: 1s\n```\n\n### Issue 5: Timeout Still Returns 500 Instead of 504\n\n**Cause**: Using v1.30 behavior expectation\n\n**Check**:\n```\nVerify Envoy version is actually v1.31:\n$ envoy --version\n```\n\n**Verify Status Code**:\n```yaml\next_proc:\n  message_timeout: 100ms\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: slow_service\n\n# With slow service:\n# v1.30: Returns 500 Internal Server Error\n# v1.31: Returns 504 Gateway Timeout\n```\n\n**Solution**: Update downstream error handling to expect 504:\n```python\n# Before v1.31\nif status == 500:  # Could be ext_proc timeout\n    retry_with_backoff()\n\n# After v1.31\nif status == 504:  # Gateway Timeout (ext_proc specific)\n    retry_with_backoff()\nif status == 500:  # Other server errors\n    alert_ops()\n```\n\n---\n\n## Field Reference\n\n### ExternalProcessor Message Fields (v1.31)\n\n| Field | Number | Type | Default | Status | Notes |\n|-------|--------|------|---------|--------|-------|\n| `grpc_service` | 1 | GrpcService | - | Required | External processor service config |\n| `failure_mode_allow` | 2 | bool | false | Active | Continue on processor failure |\n| `processing_mode` | 3 | ProcessingMode | - | Active | Which parts to send |\n| `request_attributes` | 5 | string[] | [] | Active | Attributes to populate in request |\n| `response_attributes` | 6 | string[] | [] | Active | Attributes to populate in response |\n| `message_timeout` | 7 | Duration | 200ms | Active | Per-message timeout |\n| `stat_prefix` | 8 | string | \"\" | Active | Statistics prefix |\n| `mutation_rules` | 9 | HeaderMutationRules | - | Active | What headers can be mutated |\n| `max_message_timeout` | 10 | Duration | 0 | Active | Max override_message_timeout |\n| `disable_clear_route_cache` | 11 | bool | false | Deprecated | Use route_cache_action instead |\n| `forward_rules` | 12 | HeaderForwardingRules | - | Active | Which headers to forward |\n| `filter_metadata` | 13 | Struct | {} | Active | Filter state metadata |\n| `allow_mode_override` | 14 | bool | false | Active | Allow response to override mode |\n| `disable_immediate_response` | 15 | bool | false | Active | Disable immediate_response |\n| `metadata_options` | 16 | MetadataOptions | - | Active | Dynamic metadata handling |\n| `observability_mode` | 17 | bool | false | New | Non-blocking observation mode |\n| `route_cache_action` | 18 | RouteCacheAction | DEFAULT | New | Route cache management |\n| `deferred_close_timeout` | 19 | Duration | 5s | New | gRPC stream close timeout |\n\n---\n\n## Version Compatibility Matrix\n\n| Version | Release Date | status | Notes |\n|---------|---|---|---|\n| v1.30.0 | April 2024 | EOL Support | `disable_clear_route_cache` only |\n| v1.30.1-4 | 2024 | EOL Support | Bug fixes for v1.30 |\n| v1.31.0 | July 2024 | LTS | New route_cache_action, observability_mode |\n\n**Upgrade Path**:\n```\nv1.30.x → v1.31.0 (requires config changes for route cache)\n         → v1.31+ (continue with new features)\n```\n\n---\n\n## API Proto Files Changed\n\n### Modified Files:\n\n1. **api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto**\n   - Added `RouteCacheAction` enum (lines 105-120)\n   - Updated next-free-field from 18 to 20\n   - Added new import: `udpa/annotations/migrate.proto`\n   - Modified `disable_clear_route_cache` field 11 with migration annotation\n   - Use route_cache_action Instead of disable_clear_route_cache\n\n```yaml\n# ✅ GOOD - v1.31 best practice\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR    # Explicit intent\n\n# ⚠️ ACCEPTABLE - still works but deprecated\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\n\n# ❌ BAD - both set\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR\n```\n\n### 2. Choose Right Mode for Your Use Case\n\n```yaml\n# ✅ Use BLOCKING MODE for modifications\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: false\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n  message_timeout: 1s\n  # Processor can modify headers/body\n\n# ✅ Use OBSERVABILITY MODE for monitoring\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED\n  deferred_close_timeout: 5s\n  # Processor cannot modify, only observe\n\n# ❌ WRONG - blocking mode with huge timeout\nmessage_timeout: 60s\n# This blocks request for 60 seconds!\n\n# ✅ CORRECT - reasonable timeout\nmessage_timeout: 1s  # 1 second max per message\n```\n\n### 3. Monitor the Right Metrics\n\n```\nKey metrics to track:\n\n1. ext_proc.message_timeouts\n   - Should not increase significantly in v1.31\n   - Check if set to appropriate duration\n\n2. HTTP status 504 responses (new in v1.31)\n   - Count how many are from ext_proc\n   - Should be low (implies good processor latency)\n\n3. ext_proc.streams_started and streams_closed\n   - In observability mode: may differ timing\n   - In blocking mode: should be equal over time\n\n4. Route cache statistics\n   - Monitor impact of route_cache_action setting\n   - CLEAR = more route recomputation\n   - RETAIN = more route cache hits\n```\n\n### 4. Error Handling\n\n```python\n# Handle 504 Gateway Timeout as distinct from 500\ndef handle_response(response):\n    if response.status == 504:\n        # External processor timeout\n        logger.info(\"ext_proc timeout, may retry\")\n        return retry_with_backoff(response)\n    elif response.status == 500:\n        # Other server error\n        logger.error(\"Server error, escalate\")\n        return alert_on_call()\n    else:\n        return handle_normally(response)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Support and Resources\n\n### Documentation Links:\n- [Envoy v1.31 Release Notes](https://www.envoyproxy.io/docs/envoy/latest/intro/version_history/v1.31/v1.31.0)\n- [External Processing Filter API Reference](https://www.envoyproxy.io/docs/envoy/latest/api-v3/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto)\n- [External Processing Filter Configuration Guide](https://www.envoyproxy.io/docs/envoy/latest/configuration/http/http_filters/ext_proc_filter)\n\n### GitHub Issues:\n- [Flow Control for Observability Mode](https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/issues/33319)\n- [ext_proc Filter Source Code](https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/tree/v1.31.0/source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc)\n\n### Community:\n- [Envoy Slack](https://envoyproxy.io/community/)\n- [Envoy Security Mailing List](https://lists.cncf.io/g/envoy-security)\n- [GitHub Discussions](https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/discussions)\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe v1.31 migration of the external processing filter introduces valuable enhancements while maintaining backward compatibility through deprecation warnings. This migration guide covers the changes from Envoy v1.30.0 (April 2024) to v1.31.0 (July 2024).\n\n**Key Changes Summary:**\n- New `route_cache_action` field provides flexible route cache management\n- Introduction of `observability_mode` for non-blocking external processor communication\n- Support for `deferred_close_timeout` to manage gRPC stream lifecycle in observability mode\n- Breaking change: `disable_clear_route_cache` is now promoted into a oneof with `route_cache_action`\n- Behavioral change: Timeout errors now return 504 Gateway Timeout instead of 500 Internal Server Error\n\n---\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n### 1. Route Cache Management Field Promotion\n\n**Impact**: Configurations using `disable_clear_route_cache` with non-default values alongside `route_cache_action` will fail validation.\n\n**What Changed:**\n- The `disable_clear_route_cache` (field 11) field is now being promoted into a oneof group called `clear_route_cache_type`\n- A new field `route_cache_action` (field 18) is introduced as the preferred way to manage route cache behavior\n- Only ONE of these fields can be set to a non-default value\n\n**Proto Definition (v1.31):**\n\n```protobuf\nmessage ExternalProcessor {\n  // NEW: RouteCacheAction enum\n  enum RouteCacheAction {\n    DEFAULT = 0;      // Default behavior - clear cache only when set in response\n    CLEAR = 1;        // Always clear route cache\n    RETAIN = 2;       // Never clear route cache\n  }\n\n  // DEPRECATED (but still functional): Sets route cache action to RETAIN\n  bool disable_clear_route_cache = 11\n      [(udpa.annotations.field_migrate).oneof_promotion = \"clear_route_cache_type\"];\n\n  // NEW: Replaces disable_clear_route_cache functionality\n  RouteCacheAction route_cache_action = 18\n      [(udpa.annotations.field_migrate).oneof_promotion = \"clear_route_cache_type\"];\n}\n```\n\n**Migration Steps:**\n\n1. **Identify Current Configuration**:\n   ```yaml\n   # v1.30 configuration\n   ext_proc:\n     grpc_service:\n       envoy_grpc:\n         cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n     disable_clear_route_cache: true\n   ```\n\n2. **Update to v1.31**:\n   ```yaml\n   # v1.31 configuration - Option A: Use new route_cache_action field\n   ext_proc:\n     grpc_service:\n       envoy_grpc:\n         cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n     route_cache_action: RETAIN  # Replaces disable_clear_route_cache: true\n   ```\n\n3. **Backward Compatibility**:\n   - The old `disable_clear_route_cache: true` setting is automatically converted to `route_cache_action: RETAIN`\n   - The old `disable_clear_route_cache: false` (or omitted) maps to `route_cache_action: DEFAULT`\n\n**Validation Errors:**\n```\nConfiguration Error: \"disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not\nbe set to none-default at the same time.\"\n```\n\nThis error occurs when both are specified with non-default values. **Remove the old field and use the new one instead.**\n\n**Best Practice:**\n- Always use `route_cache_action` in new configurations\n- Only use `disable_clear_route_cache` if you must maintain v1.30 compatibility\n\n---\n\n## Deprecated Features\n\n### 1. `async_mode` Field (Already Unimplemented)\n\n**Status**: Deprecated in favor of `observability_mode`\n\n**Background:**\n- `async_mode` was reserved in v1.30 as `reserved 4; reserved \"async_mode\";`\n- It was never implemented and marked with `[#not-implemented-hide:]`\n\n**What's Changing:**\n- v1.31 introduces `observability_mode` as the official mechanism for non-blocking external processor communication\n- `observability_mode` supersedes the planned (but never implemented) `async_mode`\n\n**Migration Path:**\n- If you have any references to `async_mode`, ignore them or remove them\n- Use `observability_mode` instead for \"send and go\" communication patterns\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### 1. Route Cache Action Enum\n\n**Purpose**: Provides explicit control over when route caches are cleared based on external processor responses.\n\n**Field Details:**\n- Field Number: 18 (in ExternalProcessor message)\n- Type: Enum (ExternalProcessor.RouteCacheAction)\n- Default: DEFAULT\n- Applies to: Request header processing responses\n\n**Enum Values:**\n\n| Value | Behavior | Use Case |\n|-------|----------|----------|\n| **DEFAULT** | Clear route cache only when the external processor explicitly sets `clear_route_cache: true` in the response | Normal operation - processor controls cache invalidation |\n| **CLEAR** | Always clear the route cache regardless of processor response | When header mutations might affect routing decisions; ensures fresh route computation |\n| **RETAIN** | Never clear the route cache regardless of processor response | When processor modifications don't affect routing; improves performance |\n\n**Configuration Example:**\n\n```yaml\n# Force route cache clearing on header mutations\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  route_cache_action: CLEAR\n\n# Or use the legacy form that auto-converts\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  disable_clear_route_cache: true  # Maps to RETAIN\n```\n\n**Behavioral Details:**\n- Route cache action is evaluated after the external processor responds to request headers\n- The action only applies to header processing responses, not body or trailer responses\n- Setting this field overrides any `clear_route_cache` field in the processor response (when not DEFAULT)\n\n**Implementation Location:**\n- Source: `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` (lines 186-187, 213-221)\n- Proto: `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 232-258)\n\n---\n\n### 2. Observability Mode\n\n**Purpose**: Enables \"Send and Go\" mode where the external processor observes traffic without blocking request/response processing.\n\n**Field Details:**\n- Field Number: 17 (in ExternalProcessor message)\n- Type: Boolean\n- Default: false\n- Proto Location: `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 221-243)\n\n**Configuration Example:**\n\n```yaml\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 5000ms  # Optional: defaults to 5 seconds\n```\n\n**Behavior When Enabled:**\n\n1. **Non-Blocking Communication**: Each part of the HTTP request or response specified by `ProcessingMode` is sent to the external processor without pausing filter chain iteration\n2. **No Waiting for Responses**: Envoy doesn't wait for responses from the external processor; any responses received are ignored\n3. **Stream Closure**: The external processor can still close the stream to indicate it needs no more messages\n4. **Limited Body Processing**: Only STREAMED body processing mode is fully supported; other body modes (BUFFERED, BUFFERED_PARTIAL) will be ignored, but NONE mode (skip body) works as expected\n5. **Timeout Management**: The `message_timeout` field doesn't apply in observability mode since responses aren't awaited\n\n**Important Constraints:**\n\n- ✅ Request headers will be sent in observability mode\n- ✅ Response headers will be sent in observability mode\n- ✅ Request/response bodies will be sent in STREAMED mode without waiting\n- ✅ Trailers will be sent if configured\n- ✅ The external processor can close the stream at any time\n- ❌ The external processor must NOT send back responses (they'll be ignored)\n- ❌ Header mutations from processor responses cannot be applied (no responses expected)\n- ❌ Response modifications are not possible (body/header/trailer mutations cannot be applied)\n\n**Use Cases:**\n\n```yaml\n# Observability use case 1: Traffic monitoring\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: monitoring_service\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED\n    response_body_mode: STREAMED\n\n# Observability use case 2: Non-blocking audit logging\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: audit_service\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n```\n\n**Flow Control Warning:**\n\n⚠️ **Important**: Flow control mechanisms to prevent fast senders from overwhelming the slow external processor are still under development (tracked in GitHub issue #33319). Use observability mode with caution in high-throughput environments and consider:\n- Implementing backpressure at the processor\n- Monitoring processor queue depths\n- Using circuit breakers if processor falls behind\n\n**Implementation Location:**\n- Source: `source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.cc` (lines 186, 430, 657, 683, 738, 881)\n- Proto: `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 221-243)\n\n---\n\n### 3. Deferred Close Timeout\n\n**Purpose**: Controls how long gRPC streams remain open after the HTTP stream completes in observability mode.\n\n**Field Details:**\n- Field Number: 19 (in ExternalProcessor message)\n- Type: google.protobuf.Duration\n- Default: 5000ms (5 seconds)\n- Valid Range: 0ms to 3600s\n- Proto Location: `api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto` (lines 260-265)\n\n**Configuration Example:**\n\n```yaml\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 3s        # 3 seconds\n  # OR\n  deferred_close_timeout: 10000ms   # 10 seconds\n```\n\n**Behavior:**\n\n1. **When observability mode is enabled**, gRPC streams may remain open longer than the HTTP stream lifetime\n2. **Deferred closure**: When the HTTP request/response completes, Envoy doesn't immediately close the gRPC stream\n3. **Timeout application**: Instead, Envoy sets a timer that will close the stream after `deferred_close_timeout` expires\n4. **Early closure**: The external processor can close the stream earlier by closing its end\n5. **Processing window**: The external processor has `deferred_close_timeout` duration to finish processing any buffered messages\n\n**Use Cases:**\n\n```yaml\n# Short timeout for low-latency services\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 100ms\n\n# Long timeout for batch processors\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 30s\n\n# Match to external processor processing SLA\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 5s\n```\n\n**Implementation Details:**\n- Default constant: `DEFAULT_DEFERRED_CLOSE_TIMEOUT_MS = 5000` (source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/ext_proc.h:150)\n- Managed by: `ThreadLocalStreamManager` class for per-stream lifecycle management\n- Triggered in: `DeferredDeletableStream::deferredClose()` method\n\n---\n\n## Configuration Updates\n\n### Complete Configuration Example: v1.30 → v1.31\n\n**v1.30 Configuration:**\n\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n      response_header_mode: SEND\n      request_body_mode: BUFFERED\n    failure_mode_allow: false\n    message_timeout: 200ms\n    disable_clear_route_cache: true\n    stat_prefix: \"my_ext_proc_\"\n```\n\n**v1.31 Configuration (Recommended):**\n\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n      response_header_mode: SEND\n      request_body_mode: BUFFERED\n    failure_mode_allow: false\n    message_timeout: 200ms\n    route_cache_action: RETAIN          # Changed from disable_clear_route_cache\n    stat_prefix: \"my_ext_proc_\"\n    # Optional: new features in v1.31\n    # observability_mode: false         # Defaults to false (blocking mode)\n    # deferred_close_timeout: 5000ms    # Defaults to 5 seconds\n```\n\n**v1.31 Configuration (with Observability Mode):**\n\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n- name: envoy.filters.http.ext_proc\n  typed_config:\n    \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.ext_proc.v3.ExternalProcessor\n    grpc_service:\n      envoy_grpc:\n        cluster_name: ext_proc_service\n    processing_mode:\n      request_header_mode: SEND\n      response_header_mode: SEND\n      request_body_mode: STREAMED       # STREAMED when using observability mode\n    failure_mode_allow: false\n    observability_mode: true             # Enable observability/audit mode\n    deferred_close_timeout: 3s            # Custom timeout\n    stat_prefix: \"audit_proc_\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Behavioral Changes\n\n### 1. Timeout Error Status Code\n\n**Change**: Timeout errors in external processor now return **504 Gateway Timeout** instead of **500 Internal Server Error**.\n\n**Impact**:\n- Clients can distinguish between ext_proc timeouts and other server errors\n- Load balancers can handle 504 differently (retry, failover, etc.)\n- Better observability and error tracking\n\n**Example:**\n\n```\nv1.30 Behavior: ext_proc timeout → 500 Internal Server Error\nv1.31 Behavior: ext_proc timeout → 504 Gateway Timeout\n```\n\n**Affected Scenarios:**\n- Request headers timeout while waiting for processor response\n- Request body timeout\n- Response headers timeout\n- Response body timeout\n\n**Log/Metric Changes:**\n- The metric `ext_proc.message_timeouts` counter remains the same\n- HTTP status code in access logs will change to 504\n\n---\n\n### 2. gRPC Tracing Context Propagation\n\n**Change** (Minor): Tracing context headers are now properly propagated in bidirectional gRPC streams.\n\n**Context**: Both Envoy gRPC and Google C++ gRPC clients now propagate tracing context when calling external services like ext_proc.\n\n**Impact on ext_proc**:\n- Tracing spans from the external processor request can now be correlated with the main request trace\n- Better observability when using distributed tracing\n- External processor traces will show up in trace collection systems\n\n---\n\n## Migration Steps\n\n### Step 1: Review Current Configuration\n\nCheck if your configuration uses `disable_clear_route_cache`:\n\n```bash\n# Search for disable_clear_route_cache in your config\ngrep -r \"disable_clear_route_cache\" /path/to/configs/\n```\n\n### Step 2: Update Route Cache Management\n\n**If using `disable_clear_route_cache: true`:**\n```diff\n- disable_clear_route_cache: true\n+ route_cache_action: RETAIN\n```\n\n**If using `disable_clear_route_cache: false` or omitting it:**\n```yaml\n# No change needed, but explicitly setting is clearer:\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT\n```\n\n### Step 3: Plan for New Features\n\nDecide if your use case benefits from the new features:\n\n- **Observability Mode**: Do you have monitoring/audit requirements? Enable with `observability_mode: true`\n- **Timeout Handling**: Are your external processors fast? Consider reducing `deferred_close_timeout`\n- **Explicit Route Cache Control**: Should you use CLEAR instead of relying on processor responses?\n\n### Step 4: Test Migration\n\n```yaml\n# Test configuration with new field\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  route_cache_action: RETAIN     # New field\n  # Keep other settings same\n```\n\n**Validation Checklist:**\n- [ ] Configuration loads without errors\n- [ ] HTTP requests flow through ext_proc normally\n- [ ] Route caching behavior matches expectations\n- [ ] Metrics and logs show expected behavior\n- [ ] Error responses have correct status codes\n\n### Step 5: Deploy to Staging\n\n- Deploy v1.31 to a staging environment\n- Run integration tests\n- Verify with production-like traffic patterns\n- Monitor error rates and latency\n\n### Step 6: Production Rollout\n\n- Roll out gradually using canary deployments\n- Monitor metrics:\n  - `ext_proc.message_timeouts` (should match v1.30)\n  - HTTP 504 responses (previously 500)\n  - Route cache invalidation rate\n- Have rollback plan ready\n\n---\n\n## Testing Recommendations\n\n### 1. Configuration Validation Tests\n\n```yaml\n# Test 1: Verify route_cache_action: CLEAR works\ntest_config:\n  route_cache_action: CLEAR\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\nexpected_behavior: \"Route cache cleared on header mutation\"\n\n# Test 2: Verify route_cache_action: RETAIN works\ntest_config:\n  route_cache_action: RETAIN\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\nexpected_behavior: \"Route cache never cleared\"\n\n# Test 3: Verify error on conflicting config\ntest_config:\n  disable_clear_route_cache: true\n  route_cache_action: CLEAR\nexpected_behavior: \"Configuration error thrown\"\n```\n\n### 2. Observability Mode Tests\n\n```yaml\n# Test 4: Request/response streaming without blocking\ntest_config:\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED\n    response_body_mode: STREAMED\nexpected_behavior: |\n  - Filter doesn't wait for processor responses\n  - Request completes even if processor slow\n  - Processor messages sent asynchronously\n\n# Test 5: Deferred closure timeout\ntest_config:\n  observability_mode: true\n  deferred_close_timeout: 1s\nexpected_behavior: |\n  - Stream closes after 1 second\n  - Processor has 1 second to finish\n  - No messages sent after timeout\n```\n\n### 3. Error Handling Tests\n\n```yaml\n# Test 6: Timeout returns 504\ntest_config:\n  message_timeout: 100ms\n  grpc_service: # Simulated slow service\nexpected_behavior: \"HTTP 504 Gateway Timeout returned\"\n\n# Test 7: Observability mode ignores responses\ntest_config:\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\nexpected_behavior: |\n  - Processor response mutations ignored\n  - Stream continues normally\n  - No header modifications applied\n```\n\n### 4. Integration Test Scenario\n\n```python\n# Pseudo-test code for integration testing\ndef test_ext_proc_v131_migration():\n    # Start v1.31 Envoy with new config\n    envoy = start_envoy(config_v131)\n\n    # Test 1: Normal operation unchanged\n    assert make_request(\"/api\").status == 200\n\n    # Test 2: Route cache action works\n    assert route_cache_cleared() == False  # With RETAIN\n\n    # Test 3: Observability mode non-blocking\n    with slow_processor(delay=5s):\n        start_time = time()\n        response = make_request(\"/api\")\n        elapsed = time() - start_time\n        assert elapsed < 1s  # Didn't wait for processor\n        assert response.status == 200\n\n    # Test 4: Timeout returns 504\n    with failing_processor():\n        response = make_request(\"/api\", timeout=1s)\n        assert response.status == 504\n```\n\n---\n\n## Rollback Guidance\n\n### Rollback to v1.30\n\nIf you encounter issues with v1.31, here's how to safely rollback:\n\n### Step 1: Prepare Fallback Configuration\n\nKeep a v1.30 compatible configuration ready:\n\n```yaml\n# v1.30 compatible configuration\next_proc:\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: ext_proc_cluster\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n  disable_clear_route_cache: true  # Use old field name\n  message_timeout: 200ms\n```\n\n### Step 2: Identify Issues\n\nCheck logs for error patterns:\n\n```bash\n# Configuration validation errors\ngrep \"disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action\" envoy.log\n\n# Timeout errors (now 504 instead of 500)\ngrep \"504 Gateway Timeout\" envoy_access.log\n\n# Observability mode issues (if enabled)\ngrep \"observability_mode\" envoy.log | grep ERROR\n```\n\n### Step 3: Rollback Procedure\n\n1. **Update configuration** to use old `disable_clear_route_cache` field\n2. **Redeploy Envoy v1.30** or pin to v1.31 with backward-compatible config\n3. **Verify traffic** flows normally\n4. **Monitor metrics** to ensure stability\n\n### Step 4: Prevent Recurrence\n\nAfter rollback:\n1. Identify root cause\n2. File issues if bugs found\n3. Plan retry after fixes\n4. Test more thoroughly in staging\n\n### Critical Rollback Indicators\n\n```\nImmediate rollback if:\n- Configuration won't load with \"cannot be set to none-default at the same time\" error\n- 504 responses breaking downstream systems (incompatible with 500)\n- Observability mode preventing normal traffic flow\n- gRPC connection failures to ext_proc\n```\n\n---\n\n## Common Issues and Solutions\n\n### Issue 1: Configuration Validation Error\n\n**Error Message:**\n```\n\"disable_clear_route_cache and route_cache_action can not be set to none-default at the same time.\"\n```\n\n**Cause**: Both fields set with non-default values\n\n**Solution**:\n```yaml\n# Remove the old field\n- disable_clear_route_cache: true\n+ route_cache_action: RETAIN\n\n# Or use only one field\n# Use route_cache_action: DEFAULT  (or omit it)\n# And remove disable_clear_route_cache\n```\n\n### Issue 2: Route Cache Not Clearing When Expected\n\n**Symptom**: Routes aren't being recalculated after header changes\n\n**Diagnosis**:\n```\nCheck setting:\n- route_cache_action: RETAIN → Cache never clears (expected)\n- route_cache_action: DEFAULT → Cache clears only if processor sets clear_route_cache\n- route_cache_action: CLEAR → Cache always clears (ensure this is used)\n```\n\n**Solution**:\n```yaml\n# If header mutations should affect routing\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR\n\n# If you want processor to control cache clearing\nroute_cache_action: DEFAULT\n# AND processor must set clear_route_cache: true in response\n```\n\n### Issue 3: Observability Mode Not Sending Messages\n\n**Symptom**: Processor doesn't receive request/response messages\n\n**Diagnosis**:\n```\nCheck:\n1. observability_mode: true is set\n2. processing_mode has appropriate send modes (not all SKIP)\n3. deferred_close_timeout is reasonable\n```\n\n**Solution**:\n```yaml\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND      # Must be SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND     # Must be SEND\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED    # Use STREAMED, not NONE\n    response_body_mode: STREAMED\n```\n\n### Issue 4: Observability Mode Responses Being Ignored\n\n**Symptom**: Processor responses causing mutations but nothing happens\n\n**Expected Behavior**:\n```\nIn observability mode:\n- Processor responses are IGNORED\n- No headers/body/trailer mutations applied\n- No mode_override processed\n- No immediate_response sent\n```\n\n**Solution**:\nUse observability mode ONLY for monitoring/audit. For actual request modification:\n```yaml\n# For modifying requests/responses\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: false        # Use blocking mode\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n  message_timeout: 1s\n```\n\n### Issue 5: Timeout Still Returns 500 Instead of 504\n\n**Cause**: Using v1.30 behavior expectation\n\n**Check**:\n```\nVerify Envoy version is actually v1.31:\n$ envoy --version\n```\n\n**Verify Status Code**:\n```yaml\next_proc:\n  message_timeout: 100ms\n  grpc_service:\n    envoy_grpc:\n      cluster_name: slow_service\n\n# With slow service:\n# v1.30: Returns 500 Internal Server Error\n# v1.31: Returns 504 Gateway Timeout\n```\n\n**Solution**: Update downstream error handling to expect 504:\n```python\n# Before v1.31\nif status == 500:  # Could be ext_proc timeout\n    retry_with_backoff()\n\n# After v1.31\nif status == 504:  # Gateway Timeout (ext_proc specific)\n    retry_with_backoff()\nif status == 500:  # Other server errors\n    alert_ops()\n```\n\n---\n\n## Field Reference\n\n### ExternalProcessor Message Fields (v1.31)\n\n| Field | Number | Type | Default | Status | Notes |\n|-------|--------|------|---------|--------|-------|\n| `grpc_service` | 1 | GrpcService | - | Required | External processor service config |\n| `failure_mode_allow` | 2 | bool | false | Active | Continue on processor failure |\n| `processing_mode` | 3 | ProcessingMode | - | Active | Which parts to send |\n| `request_attributes` | 5 | string[] | [] | Active | Attributes to populate in request |\n| `response_attributes` | 6 | string[] | [] | Active | Attributes to populate in response |\n| `message_timeout` | 7 | Duration | 200ms | Active | Per-message timeout |\n| `stat_prefix` | 8 | string | \"\" | Active | Statistics prefix |\n| `mutation_rules` | 9 | HeaderMutationRules | - | Active | What headers can be mutated |\n| `max_message_timeout` | 10 | Duration | 0 | Active | Max override_message_timeout |\n| `disable_clear_route_cache` | 11 | bool | false | Deprecated | Use route_cache_action instead |\n| `forward_rules` | 12 | HeaderForwardingRules | - | Active | Which headers to forward |\n| `filter_metadata` | 13 | Struct | {} | Active | Filter state metadata |\n| `allow_mode_override` | 14 | bool | false | Active | Allow response to override mode |\n| `disable_immediate_response` | 15 | bool | false | Active | Disable immediate_response |\n| `metadata_options` | 16 | MetadataOptions | - | Active | Dynamic metadata handling |\n| `observability_mode` | 17 | bool | false | New | Non-blocking observation mode |\n| `route_cache_action` | 18 | RouteCacheAction | DEFAULT | New | Route cache management |\n| `deferred_close_timeout` | 19 | Duration | 5s | New | gRPC stream close timeout |\n\n---\n\n## Version Compatibility Matrix\n\n| Version | Release Date | status | Notes |\n|---------|---|---|---|\n| v1.30.0 | April 2024 | EOL Support | `disable_clear_route_cache` only |\n| v1.30.1-4 | 2024 | EOL Support | Bug fixes for v1.30 |\n| v1.31.0 | July 2024 | LTS | New route_cache_action, observability_mode |\n\n**Upgrade Path**:\n```\nv1.30.x → v1.31.0 (requires config changes for route cache)\n         → v1.31+ (continue with new features)\n```\n\n---\n\n## API Proto Files Changed\n\n### Modified Files:\n\n1. **api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto**\n   - Added `RouteCacheAction` enum (lines 105-120)\n   - Updated next-free-field from 18 to 20\n   - Added new import: `udpa/annotations/migrate.proto`\n   - Modified `disable_clear_route_cache` field 11 with migration annotation\n   - Use route_cache_action Instead of disable_clear_route_cache\n\n```yaml\n# ✅ GOOD - v1.31 best practice\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR    # Explicit intent\n\n# ⚠️ ACCEPTABLE - still works but deprecated\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\n\n# ❌ BAD - both set\ndisable_clear_route_cache: true\nroute_cache_action: CLEAR\n```\n\n### 2. Choose Right Mode for Your Use Case\n\n```yaml\n# ✅ Use BLOCKING MODE for modifications\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: false\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n  message_timeout: 1s\n  # Processor can modify headers/body\n\n# ✅ Use OBSERVABILITY MODE for monitoring\next_proc:\n  observability_mode: true\n  processing_mode:\n    request_header_mode: SEND\n    response_header_mode: SEND\n    request_body_mode: STREAMED\n  deferred_close_timeout: 5s\n  # Processor cannot modify, only observe\n\n# ❌ WRONG - blocking mode with huge timeout\nmessage_timeout: 60s\n# This blocks request for 60 seconds!\n\n# ✅ CORRECT - reasonable timeout\nmessage_timeout: 1s  # 1 second max per message\n```\n\n### 3. Monitor the Right Metrics\n\n```\nKey metrics to track:\n\n1. ext_proc.message_timeouts\n   - Should not increase significantly in v1.31\n   - Check if set to appropriate duration\n\n2. HTTP status 504 responses (new in v1.31)\n   - Count how many are from ext_proc\n   - Should be low (implies good processor latency)\n\n3. ext_proc.streams_started and streams_closed\n   - In observability mode: may differ timing\n   - In blocking mode: should be equal over time\n\n4. Route cache statistics\n   - Monitor impact of route_cache_action setting\n   - CLEAR = more route recomputation\n   - RETAIN = more route cache hits\n```\n\n### 4. Error Handling\n\n```python\n# Handle 504 Gateway Timeout as distinct from 500\ndef handle_response(response):\n    if response.status == 504:\n        # External processor timeout\n        logger.info(\"ext_proc timeout, may retry\")\n        return retry_with_backoff(response)\n    elif response.status == 500:\n        # Other server error\n        logger.error(\"Server error, escalate\")\n        return alert_on_call()\n    else:\n        return handle_normally(response)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Support and Resources\n\n### Documentation Links:\n- [Envoy v1.31 Release Notes](https://www.envoyproxy.io/docs/envoy/latest/intro/version_history/v1.31/v1.31.0)\n- [External Processing Filter API Reference](https://www.envoyproxy.io/docs/envoy/latest/api-v3/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/ext_proc.proto)\n- [External Processing Filter Configuration Guide](https://www.envoyproxy.io/docs/envoy/latest/configuration/http/http_filters/ext_proc_filter)\n\n### GitHub Issues:\n- [Flow Control for Observability Mode](https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/issues/33319)\n- [ext_proc Filter Source Code](https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/tree/v1.31.0/source/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc)\n\n### Community:\n- [Envoy Slack](https://envoyproxy.io/community/)\n- [Envoy Security Mailing List](https://lists.cncf.io/g/envoy-security)\n- [GitHub Discussions](https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/discussions)\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe v1.31 migration of the external processing filter introduces valuable enhancements while maintaining backward compatibility through deprecation warnings.
